\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00001}00001 \textcolor{comment}{/* stb\_image\_resize -\/ v0.97 -\/ public domain image resizing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00002}00002 \textcolor{comment}{   by Jorge L Rodriguez (@VinoBS) -\/ 2014}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00003}00003 \textcolor{comment}{   http://github.com/nothings/stb}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00004}00004 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00005}00005 \textcolor{comment}{   Written with emphasis on usability, portability, and efficiency. (No}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00006}00006 \textcolor{comment}{   SIMD or threads, so it be easily outperformed by libs that use those.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00007}00007 \textcolor{comment}{   Only scaling and translation is supported, no rotations or shears.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00008}00008 \textcolor{comment}{   Easy API downsamples w/Mitchell filter, upsamples w/cubic interpolation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00009}00009 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00010}00010 \textcolor{comment}{   COMPILING \& LINKING}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00011}00011 \textcolor{comment}{      In one C/C++ file that \#includes this file, do this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00012}00012 \textcolor{comment}{         \#define STB\_IMAGE\_RESIZE\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00013}00013 \textcolor{comment}{      before the \#include. That will create the implementation in that file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00014}00014 \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00031}00031 \textcolor{comment}{   ADDITIONAL DOCUMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00032}00032 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00033}00033 \textcolor{comment}{      SRGB \& FLOATING POINT REPRESENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00034}00034 \textcolor{comment}{         The sRGB functions presume IEEE floating point. If you do not have}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00035}00035 \textcolor{comment}{         IEEE floating point, define STBIR\_NON\_IEEE\_FLOAT. This will use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00036}00036 \textcolor{comment}{         a slower implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00037}00037 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00038}00038 \textcolor{comment}{      MEMORY ALLOCATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00039}00039 \textcolor{comment}{         The resize functions here perform a single memory allocation using}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00040}00040 \textcolor{comment}{         malloc. To control the memory allocation, before the \#include that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00041}00041 \textcolor{comment}{         triggers the implementation, do:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00042}00042 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00043}00043 \textcolor{comment}{            \#define STBIR\_MALLOC(size,context) ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00044}00044 \textcolor{comment}{            \#define STBIR\_FREE(ptr,context)   ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00045}00045 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00046}00046 \textcolor{comment}{         Each resize function makes exactly one call to malloc/free, so to use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00047}00047 \textcolor{comment}{         temp memory, store the temp memory in the context and return that.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00048}00048 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00049}00049 \textcolor{comment}{      ASSERT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00050}00050 \textcolor{comment}{         Define STBIR\_ASSERT(boolval) to override assert() and not use assert.h}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00051}00051 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00052}00052 \textcolor{comment}{      OPTIMIZATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00053}00053 \textcolor{comment}{         Define STBIR\_SATURATE\_INT to compute clamp values in-\/range using}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00054}00054 \textcolor{comment}{         integer operations instead of float operations. This may be faster}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00055}00055 \textcolor{comment}{         on some platforms.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00056}00056 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00057}00057 \textcolor{comment}{      DEFAULT FILTERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00058}00058 \textcolor{comment}{         For functions which don't provide explicit control over what filters}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00059}00059 \textcolor{comment}{         to use, you can change the compile-\/time defaults with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00060}00060 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00061}00061 \textcolor{comment}{            \#define STBIR\_DEFAULT\_FILTER\_UPSAMPLE     STBIR\_FILTER\_something}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00062}00062 \textcolor{comment}{            \#define STBIR\_DEFAULT\_FILTER\_DOWNSAMPLE   STBIR\_FILTER\_something}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00063}00063 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00064}00064 \textcolor{comment}{         See stbir\_filter in the header-\/file section for the list of filters.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00065}00065 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00066}00066 \textcolor{comment}{      NEW FILTERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00067}00067 \textcolor{comment}{         A number of 1D filter kernels are used. For a list of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00068}00068 \textcolor{comment}{         supported filters see the stbir\_filter enum. To add a new filter,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00069}00069 \textcolor{comment}{         write a filter function and add it to stbir\_\_filter\_info\_table.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00070}00070 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00071}00071 \textcolor{comment}{      PROGRESS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00072}00072 \textcolor{comment}{         For interactive use with slow resize operations, you can install}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00073}00073 \textcolor{comment}{         a progress-\/report callback:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00074}00074 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00075}00075 \textcolor{comment}{            \#define STBIR\_PROGRESS\_REPORT(val)   some\_func(val)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00076}00076 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00077}00077 \textcolor{comment}{         The parameter val is a float which goes from 0 to 1 as progress is made.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00078}00078 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00079}00079 \textcolor{comment}{         For example:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00080}00080 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00081}00081 \textcolor{comment}{            static void my\_progress\_report(float progress);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00082}00082 \textcolor{comment}{            \#define STBIR\_PROGRESS\_REPORT(val) my\_progress\_report(val)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00083}00083 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00084}00084 \textcolor{comment}{            \#define STB\_IMAGE\_RESIZE\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00085}00085 \textcolor{comment}{            \#include "{}stb\_image\_resize.h"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00086}00086 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00087}00087 \textcolor{comment}{            static void my\_progress\_report(float progress)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00088}00088 \textcolor{comment}{            \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00089}00089 \textcolor{comment}{               printf("{}Progress: \%f\%\%\(\backslash\)n"{}, progress*100);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00090}00090 \textcolor{comment}{            \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00091}00091 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00092}00092 \textcolor{comment}{      MAX CHANNELS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00093}00093 \textcolor{comment}{         If your image has more than 64 channels, define STBIR\_MAX\_CHANNELS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00094}00094 \textcolor{comment}{         to the max you'll have.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00095}00095 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00096}00096 \textcolor{comment}{      ALPHA CHANNEL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00097}00097 \textcolor{comment}{         Most of the resizing functions provide the ability to control how}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00098}00098 \textcolor{comment}{         the alpha channel of an image is processed. The important things}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00099}00099 \textcolor{comment}{         to know about this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00100}00100 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00101}00101 \textcolor{comment}{         1. The best mathematically-\/behaved version of alpha to use is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00102}00102 \textcolor{comment}{         called "{}premultiplied alpha"{}, in which the other color channels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00103}00103 \textcolor{comment}{         have had the alpha value multiplied in. If you use premultiplied}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00104}00104 \textcolor{comment}{         alpha, linear filtering (such as image resampling done by this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00105}00105 \textcolor{comment}{         library, or performed in texture units on GPUs) does the "{}right}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00106}00106 \textcolor{comment}{         thing"{}. While premultiplied alpha is standard in the movie CGI}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00107}00107 \textcolor{comment}{         industry, it is still uncommon in the videogame/real-\/time world.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00108}00108 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00109}00109 \textcolor{comment}{         If you linearly filter non-\/premultiplied alpha, strange effects}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00110}00110 \textcolor{comment}{         occur. (For example, the 50/50 average of 99\% transparent bright green}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00111}00111 \textcolor{comment}{         and 1\% transparent black produces 50\% transparent dark green when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00112}00112 \textcolor{comment}{         non-\/premultiplied, whereas premultiplied it produces 50\%}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00113}00113 \textcolor{comment}{         transparent near-\/black. The former introduces green energy}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00114}00114 \textcolor{comment}{         that doesn't exist in the source image.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00115}00115 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00116}00116 \textcolor{comment}{         2. Artists should not edit premultiplied-\/alpha images; artists}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00117}00117 \textcolor{comment}{         want non-\/premultiplied alpha images. Thus, art tools generally output}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00118}00118 \textcolor{comment}{         non-\/premultiplied alpha images.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00119}00119 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00120}00120 \textcolor{comment}{         3. You will get best results in most cases by converting images}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00121}00121 \textcolor{comment}{         to premultiplied alpha before processing them mathematically.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00122}00122 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00123}00123 \textcolor{comment}{         4. If you pass the flag STBIR\_FLAG\_ALPHA\_PREMULTIPLIED, the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00124}00124 \textcolor{comment}{         resizer does not do anything special for the alpha channel;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00125}00125 \textcolor{comment}{         it is resampled identically to other channels. This produces}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00126}00126 \textcolor{comment}{         the correct results for premultiplied-\/alpha images, but produces}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00127}00127 \textcolor{comment}{         less-\/than-\/ideal results for non-\/premultiplied-\/alpha images.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00128}00128 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00129}00129 \textcolor{comment}{         5. If you do not pass the flag STBIR\_FLAG\_ALPHA\_PREMULTIPLIED,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00130}00130 \textcolor{comment}{         then the resizer weights the contribution of input pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00131}00131 \textcolor{comment}{         based on their alpha values, or, equivalently, it multiplies}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00132}00132 \textcolor{comment}{         the alpha value into the color channels, resamples, then divides}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00133}00133 \textcolor{comment}{         by the resultant alpha value. Input pixels which have alpha=0 do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00134}00134 \textcolor{comment}{         not contribute at all to output pixels unless \_all\_ of the input}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00135}00135 \textcolor{comment}{         pixels affecting that output pixel have alpha=0, in which case}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00136}00136 \textcolor{comment}{         the result for that pixel is the same as it would be without}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00137}00137 \textcolor{comment}{         STBIR\_FLAG\_ALPHA\_PREMULTIPLIED. However, this is only true for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00138}00138 \textcolor{comment}{         input images in integer formats. For input images in float format,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00139}00139 \textcolor{comment}{         input pixels with alpha=0 have no effect, and output pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00140}00140 \textcolor{comment}{         which have alpha=0 will be 0 in all channels. (For float images,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00141}00141 \textcolor{comment}{         you can manually achieve the same result by adding a tiny epsilon}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00142}00142 \textcolor{comment}{         value to the alpha channel of every image, and then subtracting}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00143}00143 \textcolor{comment}{         or clamping it at the end.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00144}00144 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00145}00145 \textcolor{comment}{         6. You can suppress the behavior described in \#5 and make}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00146}00146 \textcolor{comment}{         all-\/0-\/alpha pixels have 0 in all channels by \#defining}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00147}00147 \textcolor{comment}{         STBIR\_NO\_ALPHA\_EPSILON.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00148}00148 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00149}00149 \textcolor{comment}{         7. You can separately control whether the alpha channel is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00150}00150 \textcolor{comment}{         interpreted as linear or affected by the colorspace. By default}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00151}00151 \textcolor{comment}{         it is linear; you almost never want to apply the colorspace.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00152}00152 \textcolor{comment}{         (For example, graphics hardware does not apply sRGB conversion}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00153}00153 \textcolor{comment}{         to the alpha channel.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00154}00154 \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00211}00211 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00212}00212 \textcolor{comment}{// Easy-\/to-\/use API:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00213}00213 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00214}00214 \textcolor{comment}{//     * "{}input pixels"{} points to an array of image data with 'num\_channels' channels (e.g. RGB=3, RGBA=4)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00215}00215 \textcolor{comment}{//     * input\_w is input image width (x-\/axis), input\_h is input image height (y-\/axis)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00216}00216 \textcolor{comment}{//     * stride is the offset between successive rows of image data in memory, in bytes. you can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00217}00217 \textcolor{comment}{//       specify 0 to mean packed continuously in memory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00218}00218 \textcolor{comment}{//     * alpha channel is treated identically to other channels.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00219}00219 \textcolor{comment}{//     * colorspace is linear or sRGB as specified by function name}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00220}00220 \textcolor{comment}{//     * returned result is 1 for success or 0 in case of an error.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00221}00221 \textcolor{comment}{//       \#define STBIR\_ASSERT() to trigger an assert on parameter validation errors.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00222}00222 \textcolor{comment}{//     * Memory required grows approximately linearly with input and output size, but with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00223}00223 \textcolor{comment}{//       discontinuities at input\_w == output\_w and input\_h == output\_h.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00224}00224 \textcolor{comment}{//     * These functions use a "{}default"{} resampling filter defined at compile time. To change the filter,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00225}00225 \textcolor{comment}{//       you can change the compile-\/time defaults by \#defining STBIR\_DEFAULT\_FILTER\_UPSAMPLE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00226}00226 \textcolor{comment}{//       and STBIR\_DEFAULT\_FILTER\_DOWNSAMPLE, or you can use the medium-\/complexity API.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00227}00227 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00245}00245 \textcolor{comment}{// Set this flag if your texture has premultiplied alpha. Otherwise, stbir will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00246}00246 \textcolor{comment}{// use alpha-\/weighted resampling (effectively premultiplying, resampling,}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00248}00248 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBIR\_FLAG\_ALPHA\_PREMULTIPLIED    (1 << 0)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00250}00250 \textcolor{comment}{// when doing sRGB operations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00251}00251 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBIR\_FLAG\_ALPHA\_USES\_COLORSPACE  (1 << 1)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00678}00678     \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keyword}{const} stbir\_\_FP32 minval = \{ (127-\/13) << 23 \};}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00682}00682     \textcolor{comment}{// Clamp to [2\string^(-\/13), 1-\/eps]; these two values map to 0 and 1, respectively.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00683}00683     \textcolor{comment}{// The tests are carefully written so that NaNs map to 0, same as in the reference}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00684}00684     \textcolor{comment}{// implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00685}00685     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!(in > minval.f)) \textcolor{comment}{// written this way to catch NaNs}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00687}00687     if (in > almostone.f)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00690}00690     \textcolor{comment}{// Do the table lookup and unpack bias, scale}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00691}00691     f.f = in;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00692}00692     tab = fp32\_to\_srgb8\_tab4[(f.u -\/ minval.u) >> 20];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00693}00693     bias = (tab >> 16) << 9;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00694}00694     scale = tab \& 0xffff;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00695}00695 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00696}00696     \textcolor{comment}{// Grab next-\/highest mantissa bits and perform linear interpolation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l00697}00697     t = (f.u >> 12) \& 0xff;}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l01642}01642                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} max\_n = n1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l01643}01643                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} coefficient\_group = coefficient\_width * x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l01644}01644 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l01645}01645                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (k = n0; k <= max\_n; k++)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l01647}01647                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} c;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l01648}01648                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} out\_pixel\_index = k * channels;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l01649}01649                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} coefficient = horizontal\_coefficients[coefficient\_group + k -\/ n0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l01650}01650                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (c = 0; c < channels; c++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l01651}01651                         output\_buffer[out\_pixel\_index + c] += decode\_buffer[in\_pixel\_index + c] * coefficient;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l01652}01652                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l01653}01653             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image__resize_8h_source_l01654}01654             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
